### Level 0 - Foundational

#### Exploding Snap

A popular wizarding card game in the Harry Potter universe where cards explode in players’ hands, requiring quick reflexes and concentration.

**Tags:** Harry Potter, wizarding games, culture, games, wizarding culture

**Related:** Harry Potter

#### Unconscious (magical context)

A state induced by magical spells or hexes in the Harry Potter universe where an individual is rendered temporarily unconscious or incapacitated.

#### Jelly-Legs Hex

A hex that causes the victim’s legs to wobble uncontrollably, impeding their ability to stand or walk, used in the Harry Potter universe.

**Also known as:** Jelly-Legs

**Tags:** Harry Potter, magic, hexes

A hex that causes painful boils to appear on the skin of the target, used as a curse in the Harry Potter series.

Visual or auditory manifestations of previous spells' victims that appear as shadows or echoes when the Priori Incantatem effect is active.

**Also known as:** Reverse Echo

**Related:** Cedric Diggory’s Echo, Priori Incantatem

#### Priori Incantatem

A magical phenomenon occurring when two wands sharing the same core are forced to duel, causing a reversal or echo effect where prior spells cast emerge from the wand.

**Also known as:** Reverse Spell Effect

**Tags:** magic, wands, spells, wand lore, spell interaction, magical phenomena, Harry Potter lore

**Related:** Voldemort’s Wand, Echoes of the Past

#### Memory Modification (Wizarding punishment)

A magical procedure used to alter or erase a person's memories, often employed by the Ministry for witness protection or punishment.

**Also known as:** Memory charm, Memory spell

**Tags:** magical punishment, magic spells, wizarding law enforcement

**Prerequisites:** Obliviator

**Related:** Obliviate

---

#### Master (House-elf)

The wizard or witch to whom a house-elf is magically bound to serve, possessing authority over the elf, including giving orders.

**Also known as:** Elf master

**Tags:** wizarding society, magical bonds, House-elf

**Prerequisites:** Disobedience (House-elf context)

**Related:** Wizarding social hierarchy: Master and servant relationship

---

#### Obliviate

A memory modification spell used to erase or alter the memories of a targeted individual, commonly employed to conceal magical occurrences from Muggles.

**Also known as:** Memory modification spell

**Tags:** Spells, Wizarding World, Memory magic

**Prerequisites:** Obliviator

**Related:** Memory Modification (Wizarding punishment)

---

#### Magical scar pain

The phenomenon where Harry's scar hurts or tingles, often indicating the presence or influence of Voldemort or dark magic nearby.

**Also known as:** Scar twinge

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, magical effects, symptoms

**Prerequisites:** Common Magical Ailments and Afflictions

---

#### Curse scar

A magical scar on Harry Potter's forehead left by Voldemort's killing curse, which causes pain when Voldemort is near or active.

**Also known as:** Lightning scar

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, magical effects, curse

**Prerequisites:** Dark Magic

**Related:** Lightning-shaped scar

---

#### Triwizard Tournament

The Triwizard Tournament is a magical contest between three major wizarding schools—Hogwarts, Beauxbatons, and Durmstrang—in which champions compete in dangerous tasks to win a prestigious cup.

**Also known as:** TWT, Triwizard Tournament, Triwizard Contest, The Tournament, The Triwizard Tournament, tournament, Wizarding Tournament

**Tags:** literature, event, Harry Potter, magic competition, Harry Potter lore, events, magical competitions, magical competition, Harry Potter story arc, competition, Harry Potter universe, wizarding culture, competitions, wizarding schools, Wizarding Competition, Magic, Wizarding World, wizardry, magical events, magical contests, wizarding sport, inter-school events, magical event, wizarding world events, Wizarding events, Hogwarts events, Harry Potter series, fantasy, Wizarding tradition

**Prerequisites:** Magical Contract (Binding Magical Contract), Dumbledore

**Related:** Champions, Maze (Final Task), Second Task, Dragon Task (First Task), Magical Tasks in the Triwizard Tournament, Golden Egg (Triwizard Tournament), Golden Egg, Harry Potter, Cedric Diggory, Wizarding Schools in Triwizard Tournament, Bartemius Crouch, Champions’ Gathering, Beauxbatons Academy, Durmstrang Institute, Third Task, Champions (Triwizard Tournament), Magical Tournament Egg, Fleur Delacour, International Confederation of Wizards, Rita Skeeter’s journalism, First Triwizard Feast, Prize Money in the Triwizard Tournament, Beauxbatons Horses, Bill Weasley, Igor Karkaroff, Wand weighing ceremony, Durmstrang, Beauxbatons, Dexterous Examination Exemption, Goblet of Fire, Hooded cloak, Quidditch field, Flying Carpets, Portkeys, Dance partner, Omnioculars Slow-Motion Function, Portkey Activation, Graveyard, Scoring in Triwizard Tournament, Veela, Magical Dining via Plates, Rivalry between Wizarding Schools, Ghost of Cedric Diggory, Stadium, Ministry task force, Confundus Charm, False Attempt to Cross the Age Line with Aging Potion, Campsite, Wizarding rally, Magical Understanding, Filibuster’s Fireworks, Confrontation

#### Disarming Spell

A spell used to force an opponent to release whatever they are holding, commonly used in duels.

**Also known as:** Disarming Charm, Expelliarmus

**Tags:** Magic, Spell, Defense, Harry Potter

**Prerequisites:** Practice (Magic Training), Flitwick

**Related:** Hexes

---

#### Banishing Spell

A spell used to repel or send away objects or creatures, typically for defensive purposes.

**Also known as:** Banishing Charm

**Tags:** Magic, Spell, Defense

**Prerequisites:** Practice (Magic Training), Flitwick

---

#### Resurrection ritual of Lord Voldemort

A dark magical ceremony involving the use of Harry Potter's blood to revive the dark wizard Lord Voldemort, involving cauldrons, blood magic, and incantations.

**Also known as:** Voldemort's rebirth ritual

**Tags:** dark magic, rituals, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Blood of the enemy (magical concept), Cauldron (magical)

**Related:** Gleaming silver hand

---

#### Spell

A magical action performed by a wizard or witch using a wand and incantation to produce a specific effect or change.

**Tags:** magic, incantation, wizardry, Harry Potter Universe

**Prerequisites:** O.W.L. (Ordinary Wizarding Levels), Library (Hogwarts)

**Related:** Transfigure, Switching Spells, Diffindo

---

#### Unity

The state of being united or joined as a whole, which is emphasized as necessary to combat Voldemort's divisiveness.

**Also known as:** Togetherness

**Tags:** Concept, Wizarding World, Social Value

**Prerequisites:** Trust, Friendship

**Related:** Discord

#### Triwizard Champion

**Related:** Champions (Triwizard Tournament)

**Prerequisites:** Astrological Houses in Divination, Unfogging the Future

---

#### Wizard

A person in the Harry Potter universe who can perform magic by casting spells and using a wand.

**Also known as:** Magician, Magic User

**Tags:** people, magic, Harry Potter, Harry Potter lore, fantasy terminology

**Prerequisites:** Stunners, Code of Wand Use

**Related:** Mediwizard, Ministry Wizards, Chasers, Keeper, Seeker, Beaters

---

#### Quaffle

The red ball used in Quidditch that Chasers pass among themselves to score goals by throwing it through opposing hoops. It is relatively large and integral to scoring.

**Tags:** sports, Quidditch, equipment, quidditch equipment, magical balls

**Prerequisites:** Chasers, Quidditch Match Scoring

---

#### Dark Lord (Voldemort) Resurrection

The process by which Voldemort regained a physical body using elements taken from graves and loyal followers, marking his return to power.

**Also known as:** Voldemort’s Return

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, Dark magic, resurrection

**Prerequisites:** Wormtail’s Dagger, Death Eater Infiltration at Hogwarts, Scar Burning

**Related:** Aurors’ Vigilance, Possession, Voldemort’s Post-Fall State, Disappearances linked to Voldemort, Voldemort’s ascent to power, Dark Lord’s Increasing Strength, Dark Order, Lord Voldemort's Wand

---

#### Quidditch

A popular wizarding sport played on broomsticks, involving teams competing to score points using balls such as the Quaffle, Bludgers, and the Golden Snitch. It is played internationally and governed by officials.

**Also known as:** Wizarding sport

**Tags:** sports, magic, wizarding world, wizarding sports, Harry Potter, game, Harry Potter series, wizarding culture, Harry Potter universe, fictional, fantasy sports, magical sport, sport, Harry Potter sports, magical games, wizardry, magical world, fantasy

**Prerequisites:** Hawkshead Attacking Formation, Porskoff Ploy, Broomsticks

**Related:** Bulgarian National Quidditch Team, Irish National Quidditch Team, Snitches, Beater (Quidditch), Quidditch robes, Firebolt Broomstick, Viktor Krum, Feint, Referee (Chairwizard) Hassan Mostafa, Leprechauns (Quidditch mascots)

---

#### Death Eater

Followers of the Dark Lord who bear the Dark Mark and carry out his orders, often involved in dark magic and acts of terror within the wizarding world.

**Also known as:** Dark wizard/follower, Dark Lord's follower, Voldemort's supporter, Dark Wizard Follower

**Tags:** dark magic, wizarding factions, Harry Potter, Dark Army, Villains, Wizarding World, Magic, Fictional Character, Character, wizardry, dark arts, magical groups

**Prerequisites:** Lucius Malfoy, The Lestranges, Macnair, Nott

**Related:** Lucius Malfoy, The Lestranges, Macnair, Nott, Prejudice against giants

---

#### First Task of Triwizard Tournament

The opening challenge of the Triwizard Tournament which requires champions to retrieve their golden egg from a dragon guarding it, testing bravery and flying skill.

**Also known as:** First task

**Tags:** Magical Challenge, Tournament Task, Dragon

**Prerequisites:** Flying (magical broomstick flying), Clue in the Golden Egg, Champion, Hungarian Horntail, Magical Charm

**Related:** Death in the face, Summoning Charm (Accio)

---

### Level 2 - Intermediate

#### Protection via Harry’s Blood

Using Harry Potter's blood in the potion to resurrect Voldemort allowed Voldemort to bypass the protective magic his mother originally cast, enabling him to touch Harry physically.

**Tags:** magic, protective spells, dark magic

**Prerequisites:** Sacrificial Protection

---

#### Waterborne Hostages

Individuals captured and held underwater, requiring specialized rescue involving cutting restraints and underwater swimming adaptations.

**Tags:** emergency response, hostage situation, fantasy

**Prerequisites:** Underwater Rescue

**Related:** Magical Time Limit (Song)

---

#### Transformation Reversion from Polyjuice Potion

The process by which the real Moody’s appearance returned as the Polyjuice Potion wore off, revealing his true face, leg, and magical eye.

**Tags:** Harry Potter, Polyjuice Potion, Transformation

**Prerequisites:** Polyjuice Potion Usage by Impostor

**Related:** Mad-Eye Moody

---

#### Magical Water Plants of the Mediterranean

A book containing knowledge about underwater plants, including information that could have helped Harry in the second task.

**Tags:** Harry Potter, Magic Books, Magical Plants, Herbology, Magical botany, Wizarding literature

**Prerequisites:** Second Task

---

#### House Virtues

The defining traits valued by each Hogwarts house: bravery for Gryffindor, intelligence for Ravenclaw, hard work for Hufflepuff, and ambition for Slytherin.

**Also known as:** House Values, House Qualities

**Tags:** Harry Potter, Hogwarts, Character Traits, House Identity

**Prerequisites:** Sorting Ceremony

**Related:** Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry, House Points

---

#### Champion (Triwizard Tournament)

A wizard or witch chosen by the Goblet of Fire to represent their school in the Triwizard Tournament, undertaking several challenging magical tasks.

**Also known as:** Tournament Champion, Triwizard champion

**Tags:** Magic, Competition, Wizarding Tournament, Harry Potter universe, Triwizard Tournament, competitors, role, magical competition

**Prerequisites:** First Task of the Triwizard Tournament

**Related:** Support Cedric Diggory Badge

---

#### Magical Transport via Fire

A magical method of transportation where wizards step into magical flames and vanish to a destination, often the Burrow.

**Also known as:** Apparition through Fire

**Tags:** magic, transportation, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Magical Flames

**Related:** Apparating

---

#### Lightning-shaped scar

A distinctive scar on Harry Potter's forehead, shaped like a lightning bolt, resulting from a curse attack in his infancy. It is a well-known mark identifying Harry within the wizarding world.

**Also known as:** Harry's scar

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, characteristics

**Prerequisites:** Magical scar pain

**Related:** Curse scar

---

#### Voldemort’s Downfall

The concept describing Harry Potter as the cause and reason for Voldemort's initial defeat due to the protective magic caused by Harry's mother's sacrifice.

**Also known as:** Tom Riddle's Downfall

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, magic, story elements

**Prerequisites:** Sacrificial Protection, Killing Curse

---

#### Maze (Final Task)

The third and final task in the Triwizard Tournament, involving navigating a magical maze filled with obstacles and enemies.

**Also known as:** Final Task

**Tags:** Harry Potter, Triwizard Tournament, Challenges

**Prerequisites:** Second Task, Imperius Curse on Krum

**Related:** Triwizard Tournament, Dusk, Safety signals in the Maze, Patrollers in the Maze, Tree Root Obstruction

---

### Level 3 - Advanced

#### Potion of Rebirth

A magical potion created by Voldemort using unique ingredients and spells that restored him to a rudimentary, weak human-like body.

**Also known as:** Resurrection Potion

**Tags:** dark magic, potions, Harry Potter lore

**Prerequisites:** Protection via Harry’s Blood

**Related:** Important Ingredients for Potion of Rebirth, Nagini

---

#### Weighing of the Wands

A formal event in the Triwizard Tournament where the champions' wands are examined by the wandmaker to ensure they are in good condition before the competition begins.

**Also known as:** Wand Inspection

**Tags:** Magic, Event, Wizarding Tournament

**Prerequisites:** Champion (Triwizard Tournament)

---

### Level 4 - Expert

#### Mr. Ollivander

A renowned wandmaker in the wizarding world responsible for crafting and inspecting wands, including those of the Triwizard champions before the tournament.

**Also known as:** Ollivander

**Tags:** Magic, Person, Wandmaker

**Prerequisites:** Weighing of the Wands
